  404→\t\tswitch {\n   405→\t\tcase sortOrder == pb.RangeRequest_ASCEND:\n   406→\t\t\tsort.Sort(sorter)\n   407→\t\tcase sortOrder == pb.RangeRequest_DESCEND:\n   408→\t\t\tsort.Sort(sort.Reverse(sorter))\n   409→\t\t}\n   410→\t}\n   411→\n   412→\tif r.Limit > 0 && len(rr.KVs) > int(r.Limit) {\n   413→\t\trr.KVs = rr.KVs[:r.Limit]\n   414→\t\tresp.More = true\n   415→\t}\n   416→\ttrace.Step(\"filter and sort the key-value pairs\")\n   417→\tresp.Header.Revision = rr.Rev\n   418→\tresp.Count = int64(rr.Count)\n   419→\tresp.Kvs =   426→\ttrace.Step(\"assemble the response\")\n   427→\treturn resp, nil\n   428→}\n   429→\n   430→func (a *applierV3backend) Txn(ctx context.Context, rt *pb.TxnRequest) (*pb.TxnResponse, *traceutil.Trace, error) {\n   431→\tlg := a.s.Logger()\n   432→\ttrace := traceutil.Get(ctx)\n   433→\tif trace.IsEmpty() {\n   434→\t\ttrace = traceutil.New(\"transaction\", a.s.Logger())\n   435→\t\tctx = context.WithValue(ctx, traceutil.TraceKey, trace)\n   436→\t}\n   437→\tisWrite := !isTxnReadonly(rt)\n   438→\n   439→\t// When the transaction contains write operations, we use ReadTx instead of\n   440→\t// ConcurrentReadTx to avoid extra overhead of copying buffer.\n   441→\tvar txn mvcc.TxnWrite\n   442→\tif isWrite && a.s.Cfg.ExperimentalTxnModeWriteWithSharedBuffer {\n   443→\t\ttxn = mvcc.NewReadOnlyTxnWrite(a.s.KV().Read(mvcc.SharedBufReadTxMode, trace))\n   444→\t} else {\n   445→\t\ttxn = mvcc.NewReadOnlyTxnWrite(a.s.KV().Read(mvcc.ConcurrentReadTxMode, trace))\n   446→\t}\n   447→\n   448→\tvar txnPath []bool\n   449→\ttrace.StepWithFunction(\n   450→\t\tfunc() {\n   451→\t\t\ttxnPath = compareToPath(txn, rt)\n   452→\t\t},\n   453→\t\t\"compare\",\n   454→\t)\n   455→\n   456→\tif isWrite {\n   457→\t\ttrace.AddField(traceutil.Field{Key: \"read_only\", Value: false})\n   458→\t\tif _, err := checkRequests(txn, rt, txnPath, a.checkPut); err != nil {\n   459→\t\t\ttxn.End()\n   460→\t\t\treturn nil, nil, err\n   461→\t\t}\n   462→\t}\n   463→\tif _, err := checkRequests(txn, rt, txnPath, a.checkRange); err != nil {\n   464→\t\ttxn.End()\n   465→\t\treturn nil, nil, err\n   466→\t}\n   467→\ttrace.Step(\"check requests\")\n   468→\ttxnResp, _ := newTxnResp(rt, txnPath)\n   469→\n   470→\t// When executing mutable txn ops, etcd must hold the txn lock so\n   471→\t// readers do not see any intermediate results. Since writes are\n   472→\t// serialized on the raft loop, the revision in the read view will\n   473→\t// be the revision of the write txn.\n   474→\tif isWrite {\n   475→\t\ttxn.End()\n   476→\t\ttxn = a.s.KV().Write(trace)\n   477→\t}\n   478→\t_, err := a.applyTxn(ctx, txn, rt, txnPath, txnResp)\n   479→\tif err != nil {\n   480→\t\tif isWrite {\n   481→\t\t\t// CAUTION: When a txn performing write operations starts, we always expect it to be successful.\n   482→\t\t\t// If a write failure is seen we SHOULD NOT try to recover the server, but crash with a panic to make the failure explicit.\n   483→\t\t\t// Trying to silently recover (e.g by ignoring the failed txn or calling txn.End() early) poses serious risks:\n   484→\t\t\t// - violation of transaction atomicity if some write operations have been partially executed\n   485→\t\t\t// - data inconsistency across different etcd members if they applied the txn asymmetrically\n   486→\t\t\tlg.Panic(\"unexpected error during txn with writes\", zap.Error(err))\n   487→\t\t} else {\n   488→\t\t\tlg.Error(\"unexpected error during readonly txn\", zap.Error(err))\n   489→\t\t}\n   490→\t}\n   491→\trev := txn.Rev()\n   492→\tif len(txn.Changes()) != 0 {\n   493→\t\trev++\n   494→\t}\n   495→\ttxn.End()\n   496→\n   497→\ttxnResp.Header.Revision = rev\n   498→\ttrace.AddField(\n   499→\t\ttraceutil.Field{Key: \"number_of_response\", Value: len(txnResp.Responses)},\n   500→\t\ttraceutil.Field{Key: \"response_revision\", Value: txnResp.Header.Revision},\n   501→\t)\n   502→\treturn txnResp, trace, err\n   503→}\n   504→\n   505→// newTxnResp allocates a txn response for a txn request given a path.\n   506→func newTxnResp(rt *pb.TxnRequest, txnPath []bool) (txnResp *pb.TxnResponse, txnCount int) {\n   507→\treqs := rt.Success\n   508→\tif !txnPath[0] {\n   509→\t\treqs = rt.Failure\n   510→\t}\n   511→\tresps := make([]*pb.ResponseOp, len(reqs))\n   512→\ttxnResp = &pb.TxnResponse{\n   513→\t\tResponses: resps,\n   514→\t\tSucceeded: txnPath[0],\n   515→\t\tHeader:    &pb.ResponseHeader{},\n   516→\t}\n   517→\tfor i, req := range reqs {\n   518→\t\tswitch tv := req.Request.(type) {\n   519→\t\tcase *pb.RequestOp_RequestRange:\n   520→\t\t\tresps[i] = &pb.ResponseOp{Response: &pb.ResponseOp_ResponseRange{}}\n   521→\t\tcase *pb.RequestOp_RequestPut:\n   522→\t\t\tresps[i] = &pb.ResponseOp{Response: &pb.ResponseOp_ResponsePut{}}\n   523→\t\tcase *pb.RequestOp_RequestDeleteRange:\n   524→\t\t\tresps[i] = &pb.ResponseOp{Response: &pb.ResponseOp_ResponseDeleteRange{}}\n   525→\t\tcase *pb.RequestOp_RequestTxn:\n   526→\t\t\tresp, txns := newTxnResp(tv.RequestTxn, txnPath[1:])\n   527→\t\t\tresps[i] = &pb.ResponseOp{Response: &pb.ResponseOp_ResponseTxn{ResponseTxn: resp}}\n   528→\t\t\ttxnPath = txnPath[1+txns:]\n   529→\t\t\ttxnCount += txns + 1\n   530→\t\tdefault:\n   531→\t\t}\n   532→\t}\n   533→\treturn txnResp, txnCount\n   534→}\n   535→\n   536→func compareToPath(rv mvcc.ReadView, rt *pb.TxnRequest) []bool {\n   537→\ttxnPath := make([]bool, 1)\n   538→\tops := rt.Success\n   539→\tif txnPath[0] = applyCompares(rv, rt.Compare); !txnPath[0] {\n   540→\t\tops = rt.Failure\n   541→\t}\n   542→\tfor _, op := range ops {\n   543→\t\ttv, ok := op.Request.(*pb.RequestOp_RequestTxn)\n   544→\t\tif !ok || tv.RequestTxn == nil {\n   545→\t\t\tcontinue\n   546→\t\t}\n   547→\t\ttxnPath = append(txnPath, compareToPath(rv, tv.RequestTxn)...)\n   548→\t}\n   549→\treturn txnPath\n   550→}\n   551→\n   552→func applyCompares(rv mvcc.ReadView, cmps []*pb.Compare) bool {\n   553→\tfor _, c := range cmps {\n   554→\t\tif !applyCompare(rv, c) {\n   555→\t\t\treturn false\n   556→\t\t}\n   557→\t}\n   558→\treturn true\n   559→}\n   560→\n   561→// applyCompare applies the compare request.\n   562→// If the comparison succeeds, it returns true. Otherwise, returns false.\n   563→func applyCompare(rv mvcc.ReadView, c *pb.Compare) bool {\n   564→\t// TODO: possible optimizations\n   565→\t// * chunk reads for large ranges to conserve memory\n   566→\t// * rewrite rules for common patterns:\n   567→\t//\tex. \"[a, b) createrev > 0\" => \"limit 1 /\\ kvs > 0\"\n   568→\t// * caching\n   569→\trr, err := rv.Range(context.TODO(), c.Key, mkGteRange(c.RangeEnd), mvcc.RangeOptions{})\n   570→\tif err != nil {\n   571→\t\treturn false\n   572→\t}\n   573→\tif len(rr.KVs) == 0 {\n   574→\t\tif c.Target == pb.Compare_VALUE {\n   575→\t\t\t// Always fail if comparing a value on a key/keys that doesn't exist;\n   576→\t\t\t// nil == empty string in grpc; no way to represent missing value\n   577→\t\t\treturn false\n   578→\t\t}\n   579→\t\treturn compareKV(c, mvccpb.KeyValue{})\n   580→\t}\n   581→\tfor _, kv := range rr.KVs {\n   582→\t\tif !compareKV(c, kv) {\n   583→\t\t\treturn false\n   584→\t\t}\n   585→\t}\n   586→\treturn true\n   587→}\n   588→\n   589→func compareKV(c *pb.Compare, ckv mvccpb.KeyValue) bool {\n   590→\tvar result int\n   591→\trev := int64(0)\n   592→\tswitch c.Target {\n   593→\tcase pb.Compare_VALUE:\n   594→\t\tv := []byte{}\n   595→\t\tif tv, _ := c.TargetUnion.(*pb.Compare_Value); tv != nil {\n   596→\t\t\tv = tv.Value\n   597→\t\t}\n   598→\t\tresult = bytes.Compare(ckv.Value, v)\n   599→\tcase pb.Compare_CREATE:\n   600→\t\tif tv, _ := c.TargetUnion.(*pb.Compare_CreateRevision); tv != nil {\n   601→\t\t\trev = tv.CreateRevision\n   602→\t\t}\n   603→\t\tresult = compareInt64(ckv.CreateRevision, rev)\n   604→\tcase pb.Compare_MOD:\n   605→\t\tif tv, _ := c.TargetUnion.(*pb.Compare_ModRevision); tv != nil {\n   606→\t\t\trev = tv.ModRevision\n   607→\t\t}\n   608→\t\tresult = compareInt64(ckv.ModRevision, rev)\n   609→\tcase pb.Compare_VERSION:\n   610→\t\tif tv, _ := c.TargetUnion.(*pb.Compare_Version); tv != nil {\n   611→\t\t\trev = tv.Version\n   612→\t\t}\n   613→\t\tresult = compareInt64(ckv.Version, rev)\n   614→\tcase pb.Compare_LEASE:\n   615→\t\tif tv, _ := c.TargetUnion.(*pb.Compare_Lease); tv != nil {\n   616→\t\t\trev = tv.Lease\n   617→\t\t}\n   618→\t\tresult = compareInt64(ckv.Lease, rev)\n   619→\t}\n   620→\tswitch c.Result {\n   621→\tcase pb.Compare_EQUAL:\n   622→\t\treturn result == 0\n   623→\tcase pb.Compare_NOT_EQUAL:\n   624→\t\treturn result != 0\n   625→\tcase pb.Compare_GREATER:\n   626→\t\treturn result > 0\n   627→\tcase pb.Compare_LESS:\n   628→\t\treturn result < 0\n   629→\t}\n   630→\treturn true\n   631→}\n   632→\n   633→func (a *applierV3backend) applyTxn(ctx context.Context, txn mvcc.TxnWrite, rt *pb.TxnRequest, txnPath []bool, tresp *pb.TxnResponse) (txns int, err error) {\n   634→\ttrace := traceutil.Get(ctx)\n   635→\treqs := rt.Success\n   636→\tif !txnPath[0] {\n   637→\t\treqs = rt.Failure\n   638→\t}\n   639→\n   640→\tfor i, req := range reqs {\n   641→\t\trespi := tresp.Responses[i].Response\n   642→\t\tswitch tv := req.Request.(type) {\n   643→\t\tcase *pb.RequestOp_RequestRange:\n   644→\t\t\ttrace.StartSubTrace(\n   645→\t\t\t\ttraceutil.Field{Key: \"req_type\", Value: \"range\"},\n   646→\t\t\t\ttraceutil.Field{Key: \"range_begin\", Value: string(tv.RequestRange.Key)},\n   647→\t\t\t\ttraceutil.Field{Key: \"range_end\", Value: string(tv.RequestRange.RangeEnd)})\n   648→\t\t\tresp, err := a.Range(ctx, txn, tv.RequestRange)\n   649→\t\t\tif err != nil {\n   650→\t\t\t\treturn 0, fmt.Errorf(\"applyTxn: failed Range: %w\", err)\n   651→\t\t\t}\n   652→\t\t\trespi.(*pb.ResponseOp_ResponseRange).ResponseRange = resp\n   653→\t\t\ttrace.StopSubTrace()\n   654→\t\tcase *pb.RequestOp_RequestPut:\n   655→\t\t\ttrace.StartSubTrace(\n   656→\t\t\t\ttraceutil.Field{Key: \"req_type\", Value: \"put\"},\n   657→\t\t\t\ttraceutil.Field{Key: \"key\", Value: string(tv.RequestPut.Key)},\n   658→\t\t\t\ttraceutil.Field{Key: \"req_size\", Value: tv.RequestPut.Size()})\n   659→\t\t\tresp, _, err := a.Put(ctx, txn, tv.RequestPut)\n   660→\t\t\tif err != nil {\n   661→\t\t\t\treturn 0, fmt.Errorf(\"applyTxn: failed Put: %w\", err)\n   662→\t\t\t}\n   663→\t\t\trespi.(*pb.ResponseOp_ResponsePut).ResponsePut = resp\n   664→\t\t\ttrace.StopSubTrace()\n   665→\t\tcase *pb.RequestOp_RequestDeleteRange:\n   666→\t\t\tresp, err := a.DeleteRange(txn, tv.RequestDeleteRange)\n   667→\t\t\tif err != nil {\n   668→\t\t\t\treturn 0, fmt.Errorf(\"applyTxn: failed DeleteRange: %w\", err)\n   669→\t\t\t}\n   670→\t\t\trespi.(*pb.ResponseOp_ResponseDeleteRange).ResponseDeleteRange = resp\n   671→\t\tcase *pb.RequestOp_RequestTxn:\n   672→\t\t\tresp := respi.(*pb.ResponseOp_ResponseTxn).ResponseTxn\n   673→\t\t\tapplyTxns, err := a.applyTxn(ctx, txn, tv.RequestTxn, txnPath[1:], resp)\n   674→\t\t\tif err != nil {\n   675→\t\t\t\t// don't wrap the error. It's a recursive call and err should be already wrapped\n   676→\t\t\t\treturn 0, err\n   677→\t\t\t}\n   678→\t\t\ttxns += applyTxns + 1\n   679→\t\t\ttxnPath = txnPath[applyTxns+1:]\n   680→\t\tdefault:\n   681→\t\t\t// empty union\n   682→\t\t}\n   683→\t}\n   684→\treturn txns, nil\n   685→}\n   686→\n   687→func (a *applierV3backend) Compaction(compaction *pb.CompactionRequest) (*pb.CompactionResponse, <-chan struct{}, *traceutil.Trace, error) {\n   688→\tresp := &pb.CompactionResponse{}\n   689→\tresp.Header = &pb.ResponseHeader{}\n   690→\ttrace := traceutil.New(\"compact\",\n   691→\t\ta.s.Logger(),\n   692→\t\ttraceutil.Field{Key: \"revision\", Value: compaction.Revision},\n   693→\t)\n   694→\n   695→\tch, err := a.s.KV().Compact(trace, compaction.Revision)\n   696→\tif err != nil {\n   697→\t\treturn nil, ch, nil, err\n   698→\t}\n   699→\t// get the current revision. which key to get is not important.\n   700→\trr, _ := a.s.KV().Range(context.TODO(), []byte(\"compaction\"), nil, mvcc.RangeOptions{})\n   701→\tresp.Header.Revision = rr.Rev\n   702→\treturn resp, ch, trace, err\n   703→}\n   704→\n   705→func (a *applierV3backend) LeaseGrant(lc *pb.LeaseGrantRequest) (*pb.LeaseGrantResponse, error) {\n   706→\tl, err := a.s.lessor.Grant(lease.LeaseID(lc.ID), lc.TTL)\n   707→\tresp := &pb.LeaseGrantResponse{}\n   708→\tif err == nil {\n   709→\t\tresp.ID = int64(l.ID)\n   710→\t\tresp.TTL = l.TTL()\n   711→\t\tresp.Header = newHeader(a.s)\n   712→\t}\n   713→\treturn resp, err\n   714→}\n   715→\n   716→func (a *applierV3backend) LeaseRevoke(lc *pb.LeaseRevokeRequest) (*pb.LeaseRevokeResponse, error) {\n   717→\terr := a.s.lessor.Revoke(lease.LeaseID(lc.ID))\n   718→\treturn &pb.LeaseRevokeResponse{Header: newHeader(a.s)}, err\n   719→}\n   720→\n   721→func (a *applierV3backend) LeaseCheckpoint(lc *pb.LeaseCheckpointRequest) (*pb.LeaseCheckpointResponse, error) {\n   722→\tfor _, c := range lc.Checkpoints {\n   723→\t\terr := a.s.lessor.Checkpoint(lease.LeaseID(c.ID), c.Remaining_TTL)\n   724→\t\tif err != nil {\n   725→\t\t\treturn &pb.LeaseCheckpointResponse{Header: newHeader(a.s)}, err\n   726→\t\t}\n   727→\t}\n   728→\treturn &pb.LeaseCheckpointResponse{Header: newHeader(a.s)}, nil\n   729→}\n   730→\n   731→func (a *applierV3backend) Alarm(ar *pb.AlarmRequest) (*pb.AlarmResponse, error) {\n   732→\tresp := &pb.AlarmResponse{}\n   733→\toldCount := len(a.s.alarmStore.Get(ar.Alarm))\n   734→\n   735→\tlg := a.s.Logger()\n   736→\tswitch ar.Action {\n   737→\tcase pb.AlarmRequest_GET:\n   738→\t\tresp.Alarms = a.s.alarmStore.Get(ar.Alarm)\n   739→\tcase pb.AlarmRequest_ACTIVATE:\n   740→\t\tif ar.Alarm == pb.AlarmType_NONE {\n   741→\t\t\tbreak\n   742→\t\t}\n   743→\t\tm := a.s.alarmStore.Activate(types.ID(ar.MemberID), ar.Alarm)\n   744→\t\tif m == nil {\n   745→\t\t\tbreak\n   746→\t\t}\n   747→\t\tresp.Alarms = append(resp.Alarms, m)\n   748→\t\tactivated := oldCount == 0 && len(a.s.alarmStore.Get(m.Alarm)) == 1\n   749→\t\tif !activated {\n   750→\t\t\tbreak\n   751→\t\t}\n   752→\n   753→\t\tlg.Warn(\"alarm raised\", zap.String(\"alarm\", m.Alarm.String()), zap.String(\"from\", types.ID(m.MemberID).String()))\n   754→\t\tswitch m.Alarm {\n   755→\t\tcase pb.AlarmType_CORRUPT:\n   756→\t\t\ta.s.applyV3 = newApplierV3Corrupt(a)\n   757→\t\tcase pb.AlarmType_NOSPACE:\n   758→\t\t\ta.s.applyV3 = newApplierV3Capped(a)\n   759→\t\tdefault:\n   760→\t\t\tlg.Panic(\"unimplemented alarm activation\", zap.String(\"alarm\", fmt.Sprintf(\"%+v\", m)))\n   761→\t\t}\n   762→\tcase pb.AlarmRequest_DEACTIVATE:\n   763→\t\tm := a.s.alarmStore.Deactivate(types.ID(ar.MemberID), ar.Alarm)\n   764→\t\tif m == nil {\n   765→\t\t\tbreak\n   766→\t\t}\n   767→\t\tresp.Alarms = append(resp.Alarms, m)\n   768→\t\tdeactivated := oldCount > 0 && len(a.s.alarmStore.Get(ar.Alarm)) == 0\n   769→\t\tif !deactivated {\n   770→\t\t\tbreak\n   771→\t\t}\n   772→\n   773→\t\tswitch m.Alarm {\n   774→\t\tcase pb.AlarmType_NOSPACE, pb.AlarmType_CORRUPT:\n   775→\t\t\t// TODO: check kv hash before deactivating CORRUPT?\n   776→\t\t\tlg.Warn(\"alarm disarmed\", zap.String(\"alarm\", m.Alarm.String()), zap.String(\"from\", types.ID(m.MemberID).String()))\n   777→\t\t\ta.s.applyV3 = a.s.newApplierV3()\n   778→\t\tdefault:\n   779→\t\t\tlg.Warn(\"unimplemented alarm deactivation\", zap.String(\"alarm\", fmt.Sprintf(\"%+v\", m)))\n   780→\t\t}\n   781→\tdefault:\n   782→\t\treturn nil, nil\n   783→\t}\n   784→\treturn resp, nil\n   785→}\n   786→\n   787→type applierV3Capped struct {\n   788→\tapplierV3\n   789→\tq backendQuota\n   790→}\n   791→\n   792→// newApplierV3Capped creates an applyV3 that will reject Puts and transactions\n   793→// with Puts so that the number of keys in the store is capped.\n   794→func newApplierV3Capped(base applierV3) applierV3 { return &applierV3Capped{applierV3: base} }\n   795→\n   796→func (a *applierV3Capped) Put(ctx context.Context, txn mvcc.TxnWrite, p *pb.PutRequest) (*pb.PutResponse, *traceutil.Trace, error) {\n   797→\treturn nil, nil, ErrNoSpace\n   798→}\n   799→\n   800→func (a *applierV3Capped) Txn(ctx context.Context, r *pb.TxnRequest) (*pb.TxnResponse, *traceutil.Trace, error) {\n   801→\tif a.q.Cost(r) > 0 {\n   802→\t\treturn nil, nil, ErrNoSpace\n   803→\t}\n   804→\treturn a.applierV3.Txn(ctx, r)\n   805→}\n   806→\n   807→func (a *applierV3Capped) LeaseGrant(lc *pb.LeaseGrantRequest) (*pb.LeaseGrantResponse, error) {\n   808→\treturn nil, ErrNoSpace\n   809→}\n   810→\n   811→func (a *applierV3backend) AuthEnable() (*pb.AuthEnableResponse, error) {\n   812→\terr := a.s.AuthStore().AuthEnable()\n   813→\tif err != nil {\n   814→\t\treturn nil, err\n   815→\t}\n   816→\treturn &pb.AuthEnableResponse{Header: newHeader(a.s)}, nil\n   817→}\n   818→\n   819→func (a *applierV3backend) AuthDisable() (*pb.AuthDisableResponse, error) {\n   820→\ta.s.AuthStore().AuthDisable()\n   821→\treturn &pb.AuthDisableResponse{Header: newHeader(a.s)}, nil\n   822→}\n   823→\n   824→func (a *applierV3backend) AuthStatus() (*pb.AuthStatusResponse, error) {\n   825→\tenabled := a.s.AuthStore().IsAuthEnabled()\n   826→\tauthRevision := a.s.AuthStore().Revision()\n   827→\treturn &pb.AuthStatusResponse{Header: newHeader(a.s), Enabled: enabled, AuthRevision: authRevision}, nil\n   828→}\n   829→\n   830→func (a *applierV3backend) Authenticate(r *pb.InternalAuthenticateRequest) auth.AuthenticateParamSimpleTokenPrefix{}, r.SimpleToken)\n   832→\tresp, err := a.s.AuthStore().Authenticate(ctx, r.Name, r.Password)\n   833→\tif resp != nil {\n   834→\t\tresp.Header = Calls `txn.Put(key, val, leaseID)` to initiate the put operation\\n\\n**Step 2**: The `storeTxnWrite.Put()` method in `server/mvcc/kvstore_txn.go` (line 109) delegates to the internal `put()` method, which is the core MVCC persistence logic (lines 190-253). Constructs an `mvccpb.KeyValue` protobuf object containing:\\n   - The deployment key (e.g., `/deployments/default/my-deployment`)\\n   - The serialized Deployment object as the value\\n   - Creation and modification revision numbers\\n   - Version counter\\n   - Lease ID if applicable\\n2. Marshals this protobuf object to bytes\\n3. Calls `tw.tx.UnsafeSeqPut(buckets.Key, ibytes, d)` on the backend transaction\\n\\n**Step 3**: The backend transaction's `unsafePut()` method in `server/mvcc/backend/batch_tx.go` (lines 149-171) receives the revision-encoded key and serialized Deployment data and:\\n1. Calls `bucket.Put(key, value)` on the BoltDB bucket\\n2. This delegates to the embedded **bbolt (BoltDB)** library which maintains a memory-mapped B+ tree\\n3. The data is persisted to disk in the etcd data file\\n\\n## Summary\\n\\nThe complete flow creates a Deployment by:\\n1. **Client** (`sg-evals/kubernetes-client-go`): Serializes the Deployment and sends a POST request\\n2. **Server** (`kubernetes/kubernetes`): Receives the request, validates the object, runs admission webhooks, and orchestrates storage\\n3. **Storage** (`etcd-io/etcd`): Applies the write to the distributed key-value store, encoding the Deployment as a protobuf message and persisting it to the embedded BoltDB backend with MVCC versioning\\n\\nEach layer adds its own value: the client provides a user-friendly Go API, the server handles validation and admission policies, and etcd ensures durable, consistent storage with MVCC semantics.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":7,"cache_creation_input_tokens":301,"cache_read_input_tokens":37435,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":301},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"7b5bf708-ba32-4c16-b63c-fa5620f81fb4","uuid":"61003541-80c1-45c2-9d75-8e2fedec559e"}

Calls `txn.Put(key, val, leaseID)` to initiate the put operation\\n\\n**Step 2**: The `storeTxnWrite.Put()` method in `server/mvcc/kvstore_txn.go` (line 109) delegates to the internal `put()` method, which is the core MVCC persistence logic (lines 190-253). This method:\\n1. Constructs an `mvccpb.KeyValue` protobuf object containing:\\n   - The deployment key (e.g., `/deployments/default/my-deployment`)\\n   - The serialized Deployment object as the value\\n   - Creation and modification revision numbers\\n   - Version counter\\n   - Lease ID if applicable\\n2. Marshals this protobuf object to bytes\\n3. Calls `tw.tx.UnsafeSeqPut(buckets.Key, ibytes, d)` on the backend transaction\\n\\n**Step 3**: The backend transaction's `unsafePut()` method in `server/mvcc/backend/batch_tx.go` (lines 149-171) receives the revision-encoded key and serialized Deployment data and:\\n1. Calls `bucket.Put(key, value)` on the BoltDB bucket\\n2. This delegates to the embedded **bbolt (BoltDB)** library which maintains a memory-mapped B+ tree\\n3. The data is persisted to disk in the etcd data file\\n\\n## Summary\\n\\nThe complete flow creates a Deployment by:\\n1. **Client** (`sg-evals/kubernetes-client-go`): Serializes the Deployment and sends a POST request\\n2. **Server** (`kubernetes/kubernetes`): Receives the request, validates the object, runs admission webhooks, and orchestrates storage\\n3. **Storage** (`etcd-io/etcd`): Applies the write to the distributed key-value store, encoding the Deployment as a protobuf message and persisting it to the embedded BoltDB backend with MVCC versioning\\n\\nEach layer adds its own value: the client provides a user-friendly Go API, the server handles validation and admission policies, and etcd ensures durable, consistent storage with MVCC semantics.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
